--- 帖子 #832 ---
Read the first edition Trading Chaos, incorporate the Alligator as it is a powerful trend following tool, or you can choose to use the old system, 34 5, and 13 EMAs.  Which are almost the Alligator but not as speculative.

The problem is, Trading Chaos, and New Trading Dimensions = Powerful trend following systems.  Using all the old indis, the MFI, Fractals, Thumb trades, very profitable.

Starting at Trading Chaos 2nd Edition, the first "wise man" who isn't all that wise unless you enjoy hitting wide stops on a live account, turns the system on its head into a Counter Trend system.  Which entails larger and more inherent risk.

I trade the old system, and it is still profitable to this day, many of the new indicators, the AO, the AC, are just the shifted old indicators, fractals are enough to get in early enough on a move, to not have to risk a ridiculous stop IMO, on any time frame.  If it touches your stop, get ready for potential disaster.  In a range, or too far away, you better watch that trade, you might only get 5 pips.

I don't know exactly why Bill Williams added the divergent bar, my guess is he actually didn't, but his daughter or some other influential trader added it to the system.  That opinion is entirely speculative, but the BDB stands out as a sore thumb in what is a trend following system.  Some people use it profitably, some in Bill's trading group, I know many more it does not work for.  As a tool it really seems to break down on the higher time frames.  I don't know why, the Profitunity system is a real charm without trying to pick tops and bottoms.

And again, if you want to learn how to try to pick tops and bottoms, you can read the first book and learn very deeply about the structure of the Elliot Wave.  Become an Elliotician to pick tops and bottoms, but beware, until you have a great deal of experience you will have to relabel.  I would practice practice practice until the waves scream out at you.  And when they don't, when you are forcing labels, simply don't trade.

Hope this helps, I really am a fan of this system, hell a practitioner of it, as it was the first system I really buckled down to study and learn its ins and outs.  The First Wise man, is just not a good setup.  Rather, go back to the first book and use thumb trades with MFI.

--- 帖子 #835 ---
Depending on your interpretation of wm1 it may not actually be a valid signal if it below the red line on a long and above it on a short.  It is used in conjunction with a bdb in the "gambling stage of Bill's method.  I am having more success and more consistancy with using wm3's only.  Usually taking a wm3 is clearing past a wave 5 on some lower time frame.  I use tight stops as well once it clears my entry point after say bar 2.  If it continues my way great if not I get stopped out with a 1 pip gain. At that point I look for a new entry point.  What I have found that is working well is looking for 3 valid fractals below or above the red line.  I take the fractal with the best price entry and it does not matter what time frame you use.

Bill is big on BDB's but I have had more losses than wins using them.  If I do use one I again use a tight stop if it moves in my direction and then reverses.  I have also waited for the 2nd bar to enter as many times I will get executed on a bdb but immediately reverses for a loss.

I would suggest at this point to just focus on 3 valid fractals to form first and then take the first one that hits.

--- 帖子 #840 ---
I don't see why you would want to de-emphasize the Elliott wave, as the point of and axiom behind every indicator Bill Williams uses and has developed is based on what he calls the "fractal underlying structure" of markets, which he identifies as an Elliott Wave.   More on this later, however.

Basically everything Bill Williams developed, with the exception of the BDB (Makes sense why it doesn't work as well as everything else now, actually) is based on E Wave theory.  Bill Williams is a prominent Elliottician, and quite skilled.

Returning to the de-emphasis of the Elliot Wave:

I do believe that they streamlined the system in New Trading Dimensions and especially Trading Chaos 2nd edition to take the "lumps" out of having to actually spend a lot of time learning how to trade waves.  There's nothing wrong with this, as really the indicators still pretty much work (not as well as the first edition plain ones in my experience)...But they are based upon Bill's understanding of the structure of the EWave.

Suggestions for learning the Wave, well you could get ElWave software, practice labeling and then run the software to see where you differ with the software, as it pretty accurate.  It is quite expensive software however.  Book wise I recommend two, The Frost and Prechter one and Mastering Elliott Wave by Glenn Neely, I am studying it right now and it offers practical methods for identifying where you are at in a wave using a confluence of multiple time frames  and then labeling correctly.  It takes quite a bit of practice and study however.

Personally, I tend to spot waves easiest using the 15m TF and then the 4H TF.  Anything below 15m and the 1H I am not too great at.  I don't trade only waves though, I make much use of daily pivots for my entries as well, if a currency is near a pivot point, or S&R when I am trading.

There is a lot of controversy regarding whether EWaves work, or are too subjective, but really everything is subjective.  If you understand the intricacies of a system and apply its rules well, and have a good deal of experience as an air bag on top of that; you will have more winners than losers.  I trade Chaos with EURUSD and GBPUSD, when I trade GBPJPY and JPY pairs I only use PPs and Ichimoku, I do all right using two completely different systems, but I make sure to study them as I would any other subject, and then follow them.   Really everything comes down to knowing your system, trading it correctly, money management and experience.  As everyone says, there is no silver bullet.

--- 帖子 #855 ---
Here is another useful BW indicator - a multiple time frame AO.

Add it as many times as you want to the bottom of your chart then set each copy to the time frame of your choice.  it enables you to tell what the AO is doing in other time frames with just a glance. When all of those higher time frames all have AOs that are green or red, it pretty much helps you make decisions.

I have mine respectively set to M15, M30, M60, M240 and D1.  It is handy tool for prospecting through a series of of pairs to determine which ones are of merit.

Now if someone could write and alarm that sounds when all the MTFAO are the same color....  Or maybe display them in the upper right hand corner of a screen like the signal bars indicator does...  that would be very handy.

I have also attached signal bars for anyone/everyone to look at.  I have set the MACD in my siganl bars to 5,34 5 in a reasonable attempt to get the MTF AO replicated.

As for other indicators, has anyone tried using the Laguerres (Lags) as explained by Imram Sait on FF?

There is a good measure of correlation between the AO and the Lags that we might explore.

Chaos is pretty good as it is but we should always push the envelope.

--- 帖子 #870 ---
1. No, you don't! Bill Williams says you have to see when the alligator lines are interwining for some time (alligator sleeping) and place orders above/below the fractals. If you wait until there's a trend, you'll get it on the middle or end, and with the add-ons you will be doing you'll lose a lot.

2. Bill Williams says overbought/oversold levels don't exist, so don't even worry about that.

With all the add-ons you have to do following the original Bill Williams strategy... Unless you have a special account with very low spreads I don't see anything else than daily/weekly being profitable, maybe 4 hours too. But you have to follow it bar by bar, so unless you want to look at the monitor every 4 hours for the whole day, just trade daily or trade non 24h markets.

no buy

the gator just filled out,hes not hungry anymore
http://img405.imageshack.us/img405/7...tgatordoes.png

Gator Awakes

- when after sleeping one of the indicator bars is red and the other one is green (either above or below zero)

Gator Eats

- when both bars (above and below zero) are green.

Gator fills out

- when after eating one of the bars turn red.

Gator Sleeps

- when both bars are red.

to me this is the best indicator in the forex world,very accurate,i use it in meta trader 4,(if u use meta trader 4 ,right click on the chart,select template williams)

if any of u wanna learn about this u get can free ebook on torrentz.about the bill williams chaos theory

info.  http://forex-indicators.net/bill-wil...tor-oscillator

--- 帖子 #899 ---
One of the drawbacks of MT4 is the linear scaled charts. ElWave can do both linear and semi-log analysis, so we will see how that goes.  It can also be plugged into some FX feeds and do live EW counts in any time frame.  I tried that for a while, but I prefer longer term charts and  having minute by minute stuff happening was not suitable for me.

I run ElWave and simultaneously independently do my wave count using the BW method with the 5 34 5 MACD or the AO.  Then I compare my BW count to the selected ElWave one.  If they agree, then I feel confident  that I am on the right track.  If they do not agree, then I start to check back and forth in the alternative ElWave counts until the BW method agrees with one of the counts or I stay out if I can't find a verified solution.

ElWave is purely mathematical and gives you the possible wave counts in ranked order of how each fits all the rules.  It provides an unemotional, rational, logical, mathematical count of the preferred wave structure and ranks the alternatives based on how well they fit the rules.

I look for higher time frame counts that I think are very good, then I try to trade the wave structure inside a suitable wave on a lower time frame.

Anyhow, stay tuned, will start an Elwave thread as soon as I get some other stuff done.

--- 帖子 #901 ---
The original 3, 35, 5 MACD was used to count waves in earlier Elliott Wave Software called Advanced GET.  It is just a simple average MACD.

The AO uses a 5, 34, 5 simple average MACD of the (H-L)/2  an average of the midpoint or median price of each bar.  The Alligator moving averages are also based on the Median price.

I use the AO and AC and I also like to look at the traditional 5, 34, 5 MACD.

I have just started a new thread using ELWAVE called  ELWAVE BW Forex.  I hope to post useful material there for anyone who would like to discuss ELWave and Elliot. Drop in and visit.

Alligator: There's no secret, its just what works for my personality. Thats why I believe them when they say the system cannot be exploited, everybody trades it a little differently. I spend a lot of time looking at charts and my style has emerged from that.

crghill: I dont know anything about forex, but if I were you I would trade at a level where the typical loss per trade doesn't effect you mentally, ie small. What I had to do, which is a bit contrary to their recommendations, is quantify my risk per trade based roughly on the green line, before I enter any trade. That way I know my risk(1-3% per trade of account balance). I don't take trades where the risk is too high emotionally for me. That in turn forces patience. What I am working on now is to let my profits run a bit more. The big money is made in the 1-3 extended trends that happen in any given year. Take a look at cotton for an example. If you can catch just one of those, you can earn your whole year. I tend to set profit targets based on Fib and Ewave so that has limited my gains. The trick is to know which trade has that potential. It seems to me that failed 4th transitioning to 5th waves tend to do this, look at sugar off its lows this year.

Hope that helps

--- 帖子 #954 ---
They are high risk signals because they usually are a long way from stop loss points.  One way to limit risk is try to find great angulation on a small bar or candle.  This way, you get to take the counter-trend trade at the bottom (bearish divergence bar) of the bar.  Your stop in this case would be the top of the same bar.

I also find that divergence bars often show up at pivot points.  That's a trade worth taking in my opinion.

--- 帖子 #968 ---
Special thanks to GreenRiver for discussing his method.

I'd like to add one thing.

I use only 3 indicators and use only 1 Entry method. Answer to an earlier question on entries: I make entries on m1. I try to get in early on a possible m5 trend. and then add on on m1 fractal breakouts. This roughly covers all of the entry methods of New Trading Dimensions. Well not all but near.  I've learned one thin in life, and its paying off big time, t hats keep things simple. Because M1 and M5 is too fast a place to do all 7 kind of entries this method is taking care of my a/c.  I'm just satisfied with what i get. e.g. the following chart would show this kind of pips can turn you into someone else!

My most important point to anyone here would be this. Understanding Chaos requires getting rid of Linear thinking. pip targets, %age targets, objective system approach, technical analysis all of it limits your understanding of Chaos. Chaos = Freedom. Chaos = New Incoming Information. You must learn to let information organize itself. I've found out through personal experience and observation that human mind has 2 basic problems with accepting chaos. 1. We check every new information with what we already know. That measn we have to look in to the past. 2. We always want to predict what would be the effect and possible outcomes due to this new incoming information. Chaos is half predictable and half non predictable. We must stop predicting the future and forget the past. "The past is not beneficial and Future is mildly beneficial ". IMHO as long as you dont know the power of Saddle point it will be difficult to trade chaos.

Wiseman! The technique of the latest book, which itself is about 6 years old now, is a trend reversal technique. Bill Williams does touch this entry even in the earlier version of the Home Study Course. I remember he mentions something about a stage of knowing when to break your rules. I assume he mean the advanced level to understanding of trading where you develop a feel for the market, perhaps developed intuition. But It does not mean you should not employ the trending technique of the previous books. It simply means that if you are in a choppy period or at the end of a fast moving trend,  u could employ this strategy to get in early. otherwise if you can find saddle points here and there, then trend trading is far better then reversals. as long as we "Want what the market wants" we will enjoy trading and make money at the same.

The first signal (Wiseman 1) is a DB (Divergent Bar), but this is not always the start! But good remark: the often discussed DB should only be entered with 1/5 th of the regular entry size. I think, that`s what most of those who expressed bad experience with DB, missed. The Wiseman 1 is only a small risk (due to 1/5 size and close stoploss). But if not stopped out, it will collect enough pips during its travel to Wiseman2 to make the Wiseman2 entry small risk as well.

As DB requires a final extreme acceleration (steep angulation) before that trend stalls, it is rare! Most trends just fade and with a sleeping alligator change direction to new rise of a new trend. There you got to watch out: A candle that is mainly BELOW alligator can form a buy fractal which can be met, if its high can be met within the alligator!

--- 帖子 #1021 ---
Not exactly. A squat bar is a bar where price makes a new high/low with lots of volume but not a lot of range in that movement. Not all reversal bars are squats and not all squats are reversal bars. There is however a similarity in that both reversal bars and squats can happen at the end of a trend.

--- 帖子 #1022 ---
oo ic ic.. do you know how to mark a squat bar on mt4 just like on bw chart where he has it with a blue color??

thx

--- 帖子 #1023 ---
On MT4 there is an indicator called BW MFI which displays as volume type bars at the bottom of the screen. Each one of BW's four Profitunity Windows is represented by different color coding. The squat bar is described as having greater tick volume and a lower MFI (Market Facilitation Index which is range divided by volume) than the previous bar. Williams describes it as a battle between bulls and bears, with lots of activity but little movement, sort of like the market is "squatting" before making it's next move. As Rbr trader mentioned, a squat bar in and of itself does not necessarily signal the end of a trend. It is one of Williams 5 magic bullets that when combined together almost always signal the end of the current wave. Please read Trading Chaos the first edition for a thorough explanation.

The only problem for me here is this. I understand that in the forex market volume statistics are somewhat inaccurate and not reliable, so the squat bar and BW's other Profitunity Windows might be rendered ineffective. Does anyone have better knowledge or experience regarding forex volume?

Richard

The indicator is actually just called the Market Facilitation Index and it should be part of the regular MT4 indicator package. Let me know if you have trouble finiding it.

hey all

havent been here since forever .. but thought i just jump in quickly.

i am still using this method .. also pretty profitably i would have to say. i only do fractal trades combined with the Elliott Wave though. I barely enter on div bars or anything else.

regarding the squat bar and why i never pay attention to it: in my opinion, correct me if i am wrong, it makes no sense using this bar if you have the "average joe forex account." thats because your broker will only show you the volume that goes through their desk, but the volume of all the other brokers is not shown. with that, you might get squat bars where there actually is none, or you get none where there is one. so, unless you trade currency futures through cme or have an interbank account, it doesnt make sense using it since its based on incomplete information your broker shows you.

also what i would like to add is, that this method is profitably enough without any squat or divergent bars. picking tops or bottoms in a trend following system really isnt necessary and might just cost you more than what it makes. entering on the fractals at saddle points is highly profitable on higher timeframes for me. i am more interested in following a long move than trying to casino-play div bars going against a major trend. of course, there are certain div bars (the ones occurring at the end of wave 2 and wave 4) that can be identified easier, and that work very well. but they are still a casino signal compared to what the fractal provides for you.

--- 帖子 #1028 ---
Hi Richard,

I also remember you from some time back, good to see you around again. I have been absent myself, but I have been studying various markets and been active trading-wise every single day...

In the following I hope I can give you a little bit more insight into what I know and do regarding Chaos ... feel free to ask more questions - it can only benefit the both of us and everyone who cares to read through this thread.

You correctly observed about my trading style, that I pretty much only trade daily charts. I have found it to be the most consistent and reliable timeframe that also suits my daily schedule. Plus, I remember AvidTrader, who has met Mr Williams and bought, I believe, 2 versions of the homestudy course, saying that Bill Williams recommended it makes sense to stick to the higher timeframes with this system. Signals appear at more significant levels and trends unfold clearer from those points on. There is much less noise (esp in FX) and that makes it a lot easier to know where to get in, put the stop and get out again. Daytrading has not proven to be profitable for me on smaller TFs like the 10m or whatever you would prefer. Combining this with one significant higher timeframe can give you a good idea of where the next trend is going to go.

My knowledge is based on TC2, as you correctly observed. However, I do combine it with the Elliott Wave and Saddle points (= no div bars for me) from earlier books. This way, I make sure to stay away from any gambling trades that kill too much of my equity. I dont have a problem leaving some profit on the table, waiting for those saddle points to set up and then enter for a relatively safe trade after an initial move. Especially in FX I noticed that div bars are highly vague and the concept of angulation doesnt make a difference at all. Sometimes there is angulation and the div bar doesnt work, sometimes there isnt and it works perfectly well. I wasnt able to make sense of that until now, so I am staying away.

I would also like to mention, that other markets such as stocks (that includes Indices like SP500, Dow, Nasdaq etc) and commodity markets are much better suited for this system as the FX markets. If you bother to check out some charts of those markets and the way trends behave and move, you will find that they are much more stable. What I mean by that is, that once underlyings on those markets have established a trend, it seems much easier for them to continue that trend from a chaos trading perspective compared to the FX market. I, for instance, have developed a much higher trust in those markets than the FX market. E.g. when price is right at the green line and you kind of know that the next day will be the desicion-day regarding "will I have to close out this position or let it run", the stocks & commodity underlyings can be trusted much more regarding the continuation of the trend (thats also true for Bonds). It has happened all too often to me that forex pairs didn't give about the green line (meaning: the green line just doesnt mean we are at a significant level of correction) and just go against me even hundreds of points (on the daily..) .. meaning the next day price closes WAY above/below the green line. Stocks & Commodities run much smoother in that respect.

I am pretty sure you will not find a single broker offering futures and etf's on MT4. What you do find is commodity trading via CFDs on MT4. Honestly, MT4 is a pretty shitty platform compared to what you could afford if you were a serious stock or future's trader. Tradestation, Metastock or CQG, even Ninjatrader (I am sure there are others...) are the platforms you want to trade off if you are willing to put more money into the market. MT4 is simple to deal with regarding settings and putting in orders, but it is a piece of s/-/!7 compared to what you can do, and the reliabilty(!) of the above mentioned platforms.

I dont really know why, but a lot of people are asking me about the Elliott Wave. I have not been to a tutorial nor did I have any help from outside regarding the EW counting with the AO. I just studied the book Bill W. explains the EW in and did that like crazy. It took a while until the "aha effect" set in, but now it is just automatic. I see a chart and if there is a clear wave count (you dont always know what wave you are in - from a mail from Justine Williams - I can tell you that this is even true for them) you see what wave you are in immediately. It doesnt even take a split-second, it's simply automatic. So if you dont know how to count the waves, it's simply because of a lack of studying, not because there is some additional twist to it that is not mentioned anywhere. I have taught counting the wave to 3 other traders, and they are perfect at it now.. you only have to make the effort to go through the explanation a thousand times and compare it with the live charts you are looking at right now.

Altogether it has been my experience that the FX market is kind of tough to trade with this system. It seems there is much noise, even on high timeframes.

I am always active trading Indices and commodities and have a much higher success rate there. Even div bars are easy to spot and work hella good in those markets .. I love to take them at the end of corrections in an on-going trend .. you pretty much cant miss them, even in unpredictable wave 4s.

I hope that cleared up some questions you had.

Have a good weekend, and good trading to you!

--- 帖子 #1078 ---
hi poyais,

i use the bdb and green/red line as my exit, both has pros and cons. It's impossible to identify and exit at the top or the bottom..

if you use bdb/5 bar trailing stop u wont give back ur profit tat much, but you could miss the trend.

with the green/red line, u can stay with the market a bit longer and catch the big move, but on the other side, u could give away some of the profit. it's more like "win small or hit the jackpot"

what i do is whenever there's a divergence on the ao i tend to tighten my stop (using a bdb/5 bar trailing stop), if i see a strong trend, i use  the red/green line.

--- 帖子 #1084 ---
Hi

We all know you can enter a market anywhere you like. Its the exits that would decide your profitability. having said that timing is the most important thing in trading. So we know how to time our entries, either trade off a sleep alligator (saddle point) or BDB depending on what your taste and the market conditions.

Likewise for exits we should let the market dictate which exit or should I rather say Profit Taking strategy should we employ. WE have a choice.

You can choose any one or a combination of the following. In the long run they balance out.

1. Trail last 3 or 5 candles. (Can be used as a standard exit technique in all sorts of market conditions.

2. Exit on either Red or Green Line. Chose to exit on close on red line during the start of the trend and then later on move your exit to green line.

However this cannot be used with Wiseman technique while you are trading into the mouth of alligator.

3. Exit on Divergence. This requires patience and also depends on how the market moves. e.g. If there is a runaway market, and you have consecutive green/red candles or bars you would not like to wait for divergence. Sometimes it would save you pips other times it would exit you early.

4. Trail behing 5 consecutive Red/Green Bars or Candles. This is best for any time frame but superb for For volatile markets and specially on Shorter Time Frames ie. all Intra day. This what I use the most. I also use or try to use one more technique.

5. Trail behind fractals. this is easy for me, because my AIMS Levels indicator shows it very clearly but may be as easy, visually to see using other forms of fractals.

I hope this helps.

Imran

ps: check out my Blog for one more technique, using Fib Expansion.

--- 帖子 #1085 ---
Thank you for sharing with your valuable ideas.

My current entry & exit system that employs Wiseman 2 as the confirmation is as follows.

Entry Place the pending order to buy at High of Bullish divergent bar + 1 pip and the stop loss at Low of the bar - n pips, or sell at Low of Bearish divergent bar - 1 pip and the stop loss at High of the bar + n pips. Buy at a current market price (current price >= buy stop level) or at the buy stop level (current price < buy stop level) when three positive AO histograms (0 > values) in green appear consecutively, or sell at a current market price (current price <= sell stop level) or at the sell stop level (current price > sell stop level) when three positive AO histograms (0 > values) in red appear consecutively. <-- Confirmation by loosely applied Wiseman 2. Exit Long is exited when bearish Wiseman 1 setup (with the confirmation by W2) is fulfilled - simultaneously the initial short entry is made. Short is exited when bullish Wiseman 1 setup (with the confirmation by W2) is fulfilled - simultaneously the initial long entry is made. Please note that the above is not a genuine stop & reverse system that always stays in the market. A couple of profit-taking techniques pause the routine before either Wiseman 1 or Breakout Fractal (with the confirmation by W2) makes a fresh start.

You may think this modification grossly deviates from the original BW tenet, since the counter-trend entry is no longer used. However, the W2 filter offers us a critical advantage that can eradicate false entry signals by W1 alone.

P.S.

Thank you for referring to your proprietary info in your blog, Imran.

--- 帖子 #1089 ---
Hello,

In the world of Japanese Candlestick patterns, the followings are deemed as reversal signals. Tsutsumi (Engulfing pattern) Doji (and the variants such as Hammer for bullish or Hanging man for bearish) Kabuse (Piercing line for bullish or Dark cloud cover for bearish) Harami As it would be obvious for those familiar with them, the first three patterns are appropriately corresponded to Bullish/bearish divergent bar. However, the B/D/B doesn't encompass the Harami, which is the most likely reason when occasionally B/D/Bs do not appear around the top or bottom.

May I ask your thoughts as I think it is a critical flaw in the B/D/B concept?

--- 帖子 #1090 ---
BDB is just one way of entering a market. The whole idea is actually to trade chaos. Understand the structure of the market and act accordingly. When Price moves too fast and too far away from Alligator the rubber band principle comes into play. This is indeed a reversal technique. I get impression from majority of people that after the 2004 book perhaps taking reversal trades (wisemen technique) is the only way forward. I do not agree with that. I believe, and this is what I follow even all the way down to M1, the best place to start campaigns is saddle point. A proper sleeping alligator. I find that when you take setups under the umbrella of a 4th wave the BDB, Wiseman technique becomes very useful. But in the end, as long as you see trending markets, following trend is the best strategy. IMHO>

BDB is just a way of entering the market. 80% depends on your "mind". Moreover, a BDB only becomes worth trading when all the other requirements are met, that is angulation b/w Alligator and price, which is subjective because it depends on how experienced you are in the markets.

e.g: for H4 Traders, following trends and adding on each fractal would have been hugely profitable, just look at NZD/USD, EUR/JPY, USD,JPY, GBP,JPY, and AUS/JPY. Amazing.

Bill Williams systems make perfect sense.  If you take the time to test each entry system and pyramiding system along with the various exit signals, the entire methodology Bill Williams created is extremely practical and based in plain common sense.  Just one reading of the book should have convinced any reader that Bill Williams is on the Cutting edge of trading thought.  For one the basic statement he makes in Chaos 1st edition, he says "the basic underlying structure of the market is the Elliot Wave and the basic underlying structure of the Elliot Wave is the Fractal."  He also states that the sometimes unseen structure is our own individual belief systems concerning the market.  This is one of the most logical breakdowns of how to look at the market from a practical to a more abstract.  He also developed all his indicators and systems, a system being a simple entry into a given market and not his entire methodology, are primitive and simple, yet they help understand how the market is behaving in the present moment using non-linear dynamics and chaos theory.  This means that when I am in a trade, I know exactly what is happening in the market on multiple dimensions related to crowd psychology (fractals) to information and energy dynamics to finally price action.  He even explains in "New Trading Dimensions" how price moves in relation to the balance line measuring the flow of information and its speed.  Bill Williams to me is standing on the shoulders of some of the greatest market technicians in history.  Furthermore, just reading the books by Bill Williams will not be enough.  You need to learn money management and Elliot Wave.  For money management I recommend "The Mathematics of Money Management" by Ralph Vince.  Also, study thoroughly as much of Robert Prector's materials, but also Robert Bain.  Also, it might help to study Steve Nison for Candle Sticks Education.  Bottom-Line:  Bill Williams has developed one of the few methodologies and insightful contribution to trading the markets than few today.  This should be apparent from the first reading of Chaos Theory 1st Edition.  If you don't think that Non-Linear Dynamics and Chaos Theory are inherent in human behavior as well as all natural phenomena then you need to visit the library and study some of the recent literature on quantum physics and non-linear mathematics, then you will see that we have come a long way.

--- 帖子 #1120 ---
Hi jgimenez76,

After a very short look on your charts, because is very late in my tim zone, this is my opinion, with good chances to be uncomplete:

- TC2 is about entering in the market soon, right after a trend is over. In your case: uptrend is over, Ao is still green, you enter the market short under the low of the divergence bar, SL 1-2 pips higher then the same pricebar.

From this moment all your orders must be short.

- You are still above red line but you are expecting the price heading down , so don't go long.

- Lines for the angle must be drawn from the point where the price intersects the red line.

- Second signal: three red bars on the AO, you must enter the next pricebar, but only short.

- You take all the down fractals, but only the down fractals.then you will not have 1 long and 1 short order in the same time.

- Because you never know how much the market will give you (B.W.), don't use TP, just trail manually, at the top of the highest 3 or 5 bars of the same colour.

Bye,

K. Cs.

Hi

thank you for joining us in this lovely Chaos! Since you've asked for our opinion I'd like to thank you and take this opportunity to express what I think would be the right approach.

I personally believe the market has a definite structure. that structure is EW. Every currency, stock, commodity has its own peculiar character as well. Every time frame is essentially the same still a bit different. its like the structure of the human body, we are all essentially the same yet different.

Having said that, all markets trend. if not one TIMe Frame they must trend on a differnt time frame. If they did not then the structure of the market would have changed. it can change but so far, for the past 100 years or so all the graphs/charts are still behaving iin almost similar fashion. Many people think that Bill Williams first 2 books are too old hence they might have expired or run out or something.

I consider them as the Law of Gravity. We cannot say this law is too old now and we need to have something new. It applies exactly as it applied 1000 years ago. etc etc. The structure of the market is Elliott Wave. That structure can be traded using the incredible AO indicator. I believe one can trade only this indicator, just like Bill Williams mentions in his book.

In the third book they taught us how to trade reversals. it did not mean they put an end to trend trading. In their most recent interview they said they are most certainly trend traders but they also have a good mechanism to trade reversals as well. I believe reversals is for experts who'd traded trending markets for decades.

Having said all that, i cannot comment further but I'd like to share below what my understanding of "angulation" is.

ps: think about, the blue line is where price will be when there is no new incoming information. When price goes too fast, too far away from Balance Line i.e Blue line , the rubber band principle come into force. price comes back to it like magic.

--- 帖子 #1126 ---
I think what you are trying to trade is maybe a correction, than a change in the trend. Alligator seems to go to sleep.

However, if your buy stops will be reached, there is a possibility for the market to go upwards.

1,2, I think that 1or 2 ticks above/bellow the bar at Bill Williams means a bit higher or just above, or something like this. He is talking about 1 tick on aday chart and you have a 5m chart, and 5 numbers after 0, so can be less than 10 pips.

sl - B.W. says in Trading Chaos 2 that SL should be the high/low of 3 or 5 bars of the same colour. In New Trading Dimensions he gives a few other possibilities depending on the evolution of the price, and the guts of the trader .

Your question from the chart: more buy stops above the green bars?

- First of all you had to wait to confirm that the market is going upward: 3 green bars on the AO, then

- you were anyway under the red line of the alligator

- in order to open new positions, there are three conditions: AO green, AC green, price green

ps.: what are you using the pink line for?

Slope

The best entries, other than the saddle, come when there is a very steep slope on the green line of the alligator.

If the trend is not there, entries when the alligator mouth is opening are not going to be very productive and may just expose your trade to chop.

I suggest checking the trend on higher time frame and if it is not pronounced. best to go for a coffee instead of risking money.

IMHO

--- 帖子 #1152 ---
The Fear of Trading: The left brain

Our concious brain is what creates our physical experience of life. As a survival mechanism the concious mind always looks at the darker side of life. It looks for potential problems, so it could formulate potential solutions. It wants to one step ahead of time. Since, with every trade comes the possibility of losing the lefty always looks at the half empty glass, the negative side, the problem side.

Morning pages helps with taming down the left brain, our survival mechanism. with a strategy that could easily give you 60% losers one really needs to tame Mr. left brain down a bit. To be able to look at the bright side of the picture morning pages helps a great deal. I dont know how and what happens during morning pages but doing them absolutely eases my mind. It helps with concentration and staying in the "Now". In the words of the Great BW, "it certainly helps me get to the other side".

Another thing that is useful is "Autogenic Training". For Further details I'd recommend reading the books and visiting www.profitunity.com.

Auto-suggestion and Self-hypnosis technique.

At the end of each tape in Profitunity Home Study Course Bill Williams reminds of completing The Morning pages. in fact I'd like to quote a very important bit about the importance of 3 pages/morning pages from the book, Trading Chaos 2nd Edition,p163

"This commitment is so essential that if you are not willing to make this a serious commitment, even more important that the last 30 minute of sleep in the morning, I strongly suggest that you quit right now. There is no compulsion fro you to do this program. You well may choose to go on living your life and trading that way you have always traded.  It is your life and you should make this choice."
(in a way, he is suggesting that to trade chaos, to trade differently  then you traded before and to be able to follow his technique, you must  take this on board. He gives us no choices its a yes or no)
You can see how strong this statement is.

He also says that in almost all the cases where people would fail to become successful even after attending tutorial and/or completing home study course the reason they find is that they dont do the morning pages. It is this important. I hope I understand what is written above first and foremost and the rest of us Profitunity Traders.

Starting a few affirmative statements every morning is a best practice.

All the best,

We create our own reality.

cheers

"Between stimulus (what the indicators on our charts tell us, and of which Price itself is the prime indicator of market)  is our freedom to choose. "

(Stephen R Covey).

--- 帖子 #1178 ---
Hi,

I've created a small indicator to help finding Wave 4. As Bill Williams wrote in his book, the wave we are analyzing should contain between 100 and 140 bars to have a valid reading on the AO indicator.

Add the indicator in attachment in a chart and put a vertical bar at the beginning of the move and name it "Bar1". Put an other vertical bar at the end of the move and name it "Bar2". The two parameter of the indicator are not used. You can ignore them.

The values to be set on the MACD indicator will appear at the top left of the chart.

Add the MACD indicator to the chart and set its slow and fast periods and you have a accurate way to locate or wait for Wave 4.

If the move contains 50 bars for example, it will adapt the slow and fast periods to be used to help locate Wave 4.

Actually, to determine if the alligator is sleeping, I'm checking if during the 15 last bars, there is a bar for which the three alligator lines are not in the correct order (green red blue or blue red green).

For example if on the 5th bar before the last one, if the green line is between the red and blue lines, I consider that the alligator is sleeping.

Has anybody a better idea on how to determine if the alligator is sleeping? And something easy to code ;-)

--- 帖子 #1198 ---
Regarding divergent bars, these are only important for the (possible) start of a new position trading cycle. When you are already holding positions (thanks to reverse pyramiding) you would NOT reverse those, but wait till they are stopped out - most probably in the next bar. So you will close at least 6 units. And you might place a pending order for the next cycle -starting with 1 unit only!!!!

This is my understanding of TC2ndEd -

Regards

Forex37

--- 帖子 #1201 ---
In my opinion divergent bars are the hardest technique in the Profitunity arsenal. Their probability of success is mostly dependent on angulation but they are only worth taking if the risk of the bar itself is quite contained. As for whether to reverse on a B/D/B it is entirely dependent on the situation and is quite difficult to pass a priori judgement on it. Generally speaking, it is worth reversing if we feel that we are at the end of an Elliott Wave of some kind and the AO corroborates that view.

Hope this helps

--- 帖子 #1212 ---
Assumptions: Bearish Diverent Bar, Trade sizes microlots

If you have no prior position -, place stop sell 1 microlot at wm1, another 5 at wm2, 4 microlots at wm3......

If your are already in a postition when the wm1 occurs, your tradesize will most probably be 6 or more microlots, because during the runup you would have added the reverse pyramiding way. If you would reverse your position now, you would go from LONG 6 to SHORT 6 microlots, i.e. sell 12 microlots.

But according to BW you close a position when your stoploss is broken OR when an opposite signal occurs: Close the psoition - Sell 6 microlots to go flat.

Now you have a Bearish Divergent Bar, so place an additional stop-buy for 1 microlot.

So before the divergent bar your position was 6 microlots LONG, after it is a SHORT position of 1 microlot.

My understanding. Correct me, if I`m wrong.

Regards

Forex37

--- 帖子 #1213 ---

--- 帖子 #1214 ---
I don't think your interpretation is what Bill and Justine said about stop and reverse at B/D/B. Their advise is to stop and reverse but treat the reversal as a new position. In other words if you're fully invested on the long side and get a bearish divergent bar with angulation you should close your position (in your example your 6 units of risk) but reverse only 1 unit to end up short only 1 unit of risk. Then upon emergence of the other signals you can fully build your short position. But you should never go from fully invested on one side to fully invested on the other side, especially on B/D/Bs as they are the most speculative part of the trading strategy.

As for angulation, the book and the course are quite clear in saying that it is subjective and visual as opposed to mathematical so there isn't a lot of extra information apart from developing the ability to spot when prices pull away from the alligator and give better angulation. This is a concept that I find elusive and I haven't managed to master yet but it has been said to be one of the hardest part of the whole Profitunity system.

Hope this helps

According to my knowledge and insights "CHAOS" as defined by BW is just his definition of chaos, but not identical to any other understanding of chaos in mainstream (or even Popular) science. Its just clever hype of an ordinary (but good) trendfollowing system. Just a couple of ma, macd and smoothings. No complicated math! Plainly pure, simple and elegant. But MM included!

The systems is though to use REVERSE pyramiding: In Chaos2 for example you start the most risky signal with the smallest stake ( DB = 1 microlot), your next signal would be superAO ( SAO=5 microlots), followed by XAO or fractals... BUT the the first signal AFTER SAO would be 4 microlots, the next one 3 microlots, followed by 2, 1 and sticking to 1. After each retracement (thats all a fractal is) you now add 1 microlot til you`ve run out of investable cash. You would not add after too many candles without retracemts (In the Zone).

Thats my understanding of position building according to BW.

Decreasing, adjusting and closing this position is a different story.

--- 帖子 #1235 ---
Hype is the right word. The system may be good and may work, but calling it an application of Chaos theory is a real stretch. Although BW talks about the fractal nature of the market, he does not use the mathematics of chaos. He calls a particular price pattern a "fractal", but that is just a name, and a distortion of what fractal stands for. It is a real mistake to think that you are actually using the fractal nature of the market.

In the first few chapters of his book, BW says that you cannot predict the market, that all indicators tell about the past not the future, that statistics of the past tell nothing of the future, and that past patterns have no predictive value. Then he proceeds to develop an argument for a system that violates every one of these principals. Hype, pure and simple.

That said, the Profitunity (another clever marketing tool) system seems to be profitable for many users, and I will probably spend many fruitless hours developing an EA to test that hypothesis.

You seem to be quite correct about the EA's..too bad, but maybe they can be modified. What happens in an out of sample period is what is important.

As to 6 million iterations, that depends a lot on what was being calculated. Simply optimizing one of the EA's probably took many times 6 million iterations of some part of the code. And that does not apply any chaos theory.

My PC, and most probably yours, can do 6 million simple iterations in a millisecond or so. Minicomputers and plain old mainframes that I used to work on in 1990  could also do millions of simple iterations in a millisecond, and supercomputers were even faster. Unless you know what he was iterating, 6 million iterations is not very impressive. Do not be fooled by hype.

BTW, can you describe the computations the mathematicians and physicists were making? If they are described in one of his books, please point me at book and page. I am sincerely interested, and I may have to apologize if he really used chaos theory.

The AO signal (I think) you are referring to is where three complete consecutive bars signal an entry.

--- 帖子 #1252 ---
Before I mention anything about money management, I refer you to review the reverse pyramiding concept.  In a pristine set of trades you would have a divergent candle, the AO signal, and three fractal entries consisting of 1, 5, 4, 3, and 2 contracts respectively for a total of fifteen maximum contracts.

Contracts is another name for lots.

Considering a stop loss is an executive decision on your part where you have to decide your aggression level.  Referencing the EURUSD H1 chart beginning 8/31, you have your choice of following trades with a lagging five completed bar stop loss, a green line stop loss, or a red line stop loss.  All of these are mentioned in the book Trading Chaos: Second Edition.

The Awesome Oscillator hit a peak 9/1 around GMT 11:00 indicating we were in the third Elliot Wave.  If you are a skittish trader and used the five-bar lagging stop, your trades would have been stopped out several times.  A red balance line stop loss would have kept you in the trend until 9/2.  Also there was a second set of entries until wave three gave way to wave four on 9/6.

To answer your question on money management, once you have reached a level of trading where you can spot entries and take advantage of the reverse pyramiding concept you should not leverage more than 50% of your available margin.  Additionally, your total margin risked is up to you if you choose a lesser amount.  Ultimately if you are trading the method the market manages your trades and MM.

--- 帖子 #1271 ---
Hi fellow traders,

I'd like you guys to evaluate my idea, Chikou-span遅行スパン (Lagging span in English) breakout.

For example, an emerging Up Fractal above Alligator lips in green from the bracketed market usually indicates the inception of bull market. This notion is always true in hindsight. The Chikou span gives you a clue on effectively identifying the false breakout.

Check your chart by plotting Ichimoku.mq4 after turing all of Colors except #4 Lime (for Chikou span) into None, then locate the candles where the expression of inequality below holds true:

Bullish: Chikou span (note: the latest value is shown 26 periods ago) > High price of the candle of 26 periods ago,

Bearish: Low price of candle of 26 periods ago > Chikou span.

If this is the case, your Up/Down Fractals formed above/below Alligator are highly likely to be a promising bullish/bearish Wiseman 3 signal, thus you are able to enter/add your position least stressfully.

Then, when should we close the existing positions? That's the moment the above inequalities become inadequate (when getting to the equilibrium point (Kinkou均衡)), which might be well before three Alligator lines are intertwining. However your exit must be less painful than the New-Trading-Dimensions way of exit formula where you give back what you will have amassed to the market.

Finally, please note that the Chikou-span breakout is a popular strategy for Japanese, which has proved over half a century. My idea is merely an application to the Bill Williams system.

Good luck!

--- 帖子 #1272 ---
As this thread seems stagnating, let me raise one more topic.

Can markets allow us to properly calculate the standard deviation? Unless you can substantiate it, the credibility of your technical analysis must be deteriorated down to almost nothing. Why? Because you unconsciously presume the 19th century's Gaussian distribution.

This assumption alone provides us with an enormous edge in the market.

Because now we are able to pick up trading systems or methods that reasonably work among the waste collected over centuries.

Do you make sense what I'm arguing? If not, you are most likely to lose money in the market. Read this book, The Misbehavior of Markets: A Fractal View of Financial Turbulence by Benoit Mandelbrot.

--- 帖子 #1273 ---
I'm not sure what you are saying. If you refer to the fact that markets are not stationary, I could not agree more. However, when the series is stationary, the standard deviation calculation is not dependent on the distribution. It is calculated the same way for a Gaussian distribution as for any non-gaussian.

On the other hand, the standard deviation is meaningless if stationarity does not hold. By definition stationarity does not hold if the moments depend on the time when they are calculated, or the duration of the sample used.

The FX market may be in some sense short term stationary, i.e., the moments may change very slowly w.r.t the TF in use. In that case, it makes sense to compute the S.D. and any other moments that are useful. However, the computation must use a sliding window that is short w.r.t. the time it takes the S.D. to change much. This means that the start time for computation must slide.

Also I don't see how the Gaussian assumption provides us with an edge. It is not true, and it is meaningless in the long term due to stationarity considerations. The only edge I could see is if I were trading against someone that assumed stationarity. But I don't think many traders think that deeply, or make trades on that assumption.

--- 帖子 #1275 ---
Thank you for the nice introductory explanations of standard deviation concept (S.D.).

Yes, S.D. can be appropriately computed in hindsight, however almost in vain if we apply it to the future as we see past returns are most likely not indicative of future results. The backtesting provides a good example.  The EA usually becomes obsolete in a couple of months even though it demonstrates an impressive equity curve for the last ten years. Can we always attribute it to the over-fitting issue? I think almost all of technical analysis are on common ground of this matter. We can properly calculate the S.D. for a given period in the past, but the problem is we are trying to apply the probability distributions we get in backtesting to the market in the future regardless of consciously or unconsciously. This is the reason why a seemingly promising (statistically significant at present) trading strategy is most likely short-lived and destined to throw away to the wasteland.

Having said that, it might be possible to compute the S.D. in the foreseeable future if we alleviate the assumptions to the extent not practical enough to withstand as you mentioned "if stationarity does hold," which is totally irrelevant to what we pursue.

Chaos theory offers us a clue to evade the persistent issue and how to pick up a reasonably right method to approximate the current market. How? I'll leave the answer to the aforementioned book, however please don't misunderstand I'm not endorsing the Bill's trading system but just remind the thread participants of the foundation of Chaos trading. In this regard I'd also like to have comments by traders who subscribe different methodology, if possible.

Have a great weekend!

--- 帖子 #1276 ---
I remember when Mandlebrot's fractal article on the stock market was published.

One of the readers who wrote in to Scientific American to comment on the article, pointed out that Ralph Nelson Elliott had some nerve stealing Mandlebrot's ideas some thirty years before Mandlebrot had thought of them.

I like Bill Williams ideas because they attempt to use Elliott Wave without the need to really understand Elliott Wave.

Unfortunately there are so many people who falsely claim Elliott Wave expertise (including a few on this thread) that they give the subject a bad name. Nonetheless, if you study the wave principle and use Bill's fractals and alligator you can do very well.

No curve fitting required, no magic, no standard deviations, no secret sauce indicators; just learn to count waves and read the Alligator.  Take the first fractal above or below the red line and keep it simple.

--- 帖子 #1277 ---
Refreshing.... good solid Canuck logic.

There is no doubt in my mind that markets are wave within wave within wave ...... like in nature. William's attempt to delineate this structure and exploit it is a noble one and can no doubt be profitable (as can most other methodologies) if traded by one who has a good grasp of classic principles of technical analysis. One principle (and skill) in particular is that of understanding the importance of and the ability to recognize significant areas of support and resistance. I am actually quite surprised that William's never made this an important and more simple element of his methodology as opposed to the convoluted and arcaine Wisemen concepts. If markets truely are wave like in nature then it stands to reason that certain S/R levels are going to be the wave turning points i.e. fractals of greater importance or call them super fractals, if you will.

In my humble opinion, no matter what your trading methodology, one can hardly go wrong knowing your S/R theory, after that it becomes a matter of wait and see (the letting the market come to you approach) how price reacts at those levels then trading accordingly as indicated by the Alligator et al (or for that matter, any other system).

My 2 pips worth. Thanks for listening.

I spent many, many hours hunting for an Alligator Cross alert.

I finally found an indicator that almost does the job.  Unfortunately the sound doesn't work

However, I think all Chaos fans will find this most useful and maybe some kind soul will get the sound working for us.

You can set this indicator up and it should give you a sound alert and an arrow when the Red Alligator line crosses the Blue one.

The arrows work.

Settings are:  true, false, 2, 8, 5, 4, 2 13, 8, 4

Or you can set it to alert when the Green line crosses the Blue.

Settings for that are:  true, false, 2, 5, 3, 4, 2 13, 8, 4

Land of cash is working on an entry system based on a MA shift crossover for their LOC Trader ea.  (Do a search on FF for LOCTrader.) With that, you can then choose your choice of trailing stop strategy.

In many ways it will allow Chaos traders to get an automatic entry on an Alligator Cross over and then trail a stop along one of the Alligator lines.

Sleep may be possible again if we can get the sound part of this alert working.

--- 帖子 #1332 ---
Entry level was above the HH  (higher high)  fractal that is above the red line (Third wise man I believe.)  It wasn't above the red line when it formed but the red line dipped and made it legitimate to take that level for an entry 7 bars later.

Then I let LOC trail the stop on a 5, 3 displaced smoothed median MA (The Green Alligator line) plus one pip.  The one pip extra prevents being stopped out on touches of the Alligator line.  I also set my intial stop one pip below the fractal as Bill Williams does and LOC will move it up once the trade gets going and the Green Alligator line gets above your entry level.

Once you get in a trade you let LOC manage it and it really makes trading a lot less time consuming.  Even one minute charts can take an hour or more to run out a good trade and that is an hour that you can walk away and not have to baby sit.

The Version that does this is LOCTrailingMA.  Another version, LOCTrailing, has fractal stops that also work well.  Sometimes I use an X bars back stop which it also has.

Mikhail, the fellow who codes LOC, is very decent and and added the displaced moving averages and at my request.

I am not in anyway involved with LOC beyond using it and thinking that it is great trailing stop software.  It is a great system to use in conjunction with Bill Williams methods and does a lot to solve the problem of where to exit and how to manage a trade once you are in it.

Check out Land of Cash (LOC) for some demo videos.  It is worth every cent in my opinion.

--- 帖子 #1370 ---
the indicator, which will paint the bars in accordance with evidences of the indicator MFI and volumes on description from "Trade CHAOS". attach;fasten. Use.

The Parameter whole one:

BarsToProcess=1000; //maximum amount bar for calculation of the indicator (-1 - all bars)

When aiming on bar is displayed surfacing help with explanation in accordance with book B.Williams

Index of the Relief Market (Market Facilitation Index, BW MFI)

The Indicator pays on formula:

BW MFI = (HIGH - LOW) / VOLUME

Where:

HIGH - a maximum price of the current bar;

LOW - a minimum price of the current bar;

VOLUME - a volume of the current bar.

The Signals Market Facilitation Index (BW MFI):

The Simultaneous growing BW MFI and volume (Volume) speaks of that that all more player falls into the market (grows the volume), and new players open the positions toward development of the bar.

The Simultaneous fall BW MFI and volume speaks of reduction of the interest participant to given speaker of the price.

BW MFI вырос, but volume fell   market does not support such speaker of the price. Change the price   result gamble.

BW MFI fell, but volume вырос   goes the hardened fight between oxen and bear (the volume вырос), but power approximately are (the indicator fell). Such bar B.VILIYAMS named "cowerring". Usually breakout of such bar very important with standpoint future speakers price.
http://storage9.static.itmages.ru/i/...425d8834fd.pnghttp://storage6.static.itmages.ru/i/...fc17655ac3.png

--- 帖子 #1376 ---
I suppose everyone will have a different experience.  When I first read his book I didn't quite connect with the psychological and mental points  he was writing about.  It wasn't until later and when I looked at the system in its entirety that it made some sense.

I've had profitable results, even with very small accounts I was impressed with how he laid out money management aspect of the trades.   I think other systems fail in this regards.  Other systems will point out optimal entry and indicator signals.  Not many will show you how to manage the trade and especially when to exit. The exit is sometimes where other systems get killed.  They'll be profitable, stay in a trade too long, and not only give back all profits, but sometimes take big losses.   I have an old statement on my site where I traded a micro account and consistently had a profit factor between 3-17  with drawdowns less than 10%  The first half of the year I lost half the account, the 2nd half of the year I traded Chaos, made back all the loses and doubled the account.

I did use some Elliott Wave, but the point is the Chaos Method can be traded as is, or it can be coupled with another system to support analysis of the overall trend. It can be used to trade with the trend, countertrend, short time frame long time frames, all under one consistent framework.  There is time involved, and while I like other systems that keep it simple, sometimes being too simple leaves a system incomplete and vulnerable in changing markets.

It's not for everyone, it's just a matter of whether it'll suit and fit your style of trading. Anyways, what matters int he end is results, consistency, safety and profits.

Fractals and their levels are one of the precious few objective things we can say about the markets.

with this.

structure and then use his strategy for trading it you will be on your way.

Elliott Wave theory has been in use in the markets since the 1930’s when R.N. Elliott discovered these repeating patterns in the stock markets. It has been one of the most difficult areas of the market for traders to understand. Profitunity presents the Elliott Wave theory in a simple and effective way that any stock, forex or commodity trader can understand in the new Profitunity Elliott Wave DVD by Justine Williams-Lara.

By understanding the underlying structure of the markets (the Elliott Wave) traders can improve their current trading results. Knowing what direction to expect next and why is especially valuable in today’s volatile markets. Profitunity follows traditional Elliott Wave theory and adds some of their own technical indicators to help ensure an accurate quick and simple count. If you can count to 5 and know your A,B,C’s, then you can learn to count the Elliott Wave the Profitunity way. This method can achieve amazing results and has been used in our own trading accounts for decades.

In this 90-minute course, Justine will teach you how to count the Elliott Wave with simple and precise techniques on real time charts on all time frames and markets including stocks, futures, ETF’s, indices, and Forex.

Justine will also teach you:

• What the Underlying Structure of the Markets is

• What are Fractals and how are they related to the Elliott Wave

• How to use the Awesome Oscillator to find the peak of Wave 3

• Correction types: Zig-Zag, Complex, and Irregular patterns

• How the Elliott Wave is the underlying  structure of all markets

• How the Fractal is the underlying part of the Elliott Wave

• Identify the 5 Wave Pattern with 3 wave correction on the chart on any market

• The Awesome Oscillator - 5-34 moving average and it’s uses

• How to Identify the Wave 3 peak on a chart in seconds

• What divergence means and how it affects the Elliott Waves

• The Squat Bar, trend ending or measuring are explained in real time examples

• What the common correction types are and how to recognize them on the chart

• How to use multiple time frames to accurately count Elliott Waves in real time.

• Take the ambiguity out of counting Elliott Waves

• How to know when your count is wrong and get the current Elliott Wave count.

• Review on 30 examples on historical charts tying it all together.

This DVD is packed with realtime examples to count Elliott Waves. No matter what markets or time frames you trade, new and seasoned traders alike will enhance their trading arsenal. You will fine tune your entries and exits and improve your ability to spot the trend!

--- 帖子 #1477 ---
I`m afraid, you completely misunderstood the system!!!!! The fractals are NOT indicators, don`t point anywhere. They are just the indicating the last low or last high. And the method teaches to NOT trade, but set a pending order with due distance to this fractal. So for the blue circled fractal (which is only indicated after the following two candles have finished) you should have placed a pending SELL order a few pips below the low of that candle (the one that shows the blue circle).

You would place that order at the same time when the third following candle opens ( the hammer). So the order is pending - but nothing happening with this (blue)order. At the beginning of the candle circled red you will notice 2 things: Your BLUE sell order was triggered (maybe even one day earlier) and a new pivot indicator was printed (the one three days earlier with that long white candle and pivot indicator above). So you set a new LONG pending order a a price a few pips above the highest high of that white candle (ca. 1.278x).

At the last day the red circled pivot will be printed and you place a new SELL pending order  at about 1.235x.

So you have now 1 running order (not yet stopped out, but wide profit), and 2 pending orders

Actually a nice setup. So read the books.

Regards

p.s. this was only about the fractals.

--- 帖子 #1485 ---
I am a Fractal Junky. There are a few You Tube Videos online where Bill Williams explains his Chaos Method of trading. The "Holy Grail" is the best one.

It explains what a fractal is and how they are formed. Now, I have taken his knowledge and the research that he paid to have done about the market, and added my own perks. I've thrown is some VSA , Some knowledge about Euro Trading Levels for Breakouts, and Added the Fibonacci Levels to my approach at trading. It is quiet impressive.

A Fractal is nothing more than a Behavioral change in the Market. Smart Money( high volume candles) is what makes the Fractal's behavior change. That change in behavior is headed somewhere, but where? It is headed to a Fib Level that the Market Makers and Smart Money have in mind , that's where.

There are 4 basic levels that the Euro Market Makers and Smart Money use as Breakout areas. They are associated in the last 2 digits of the Euro Price, for example 1.2100,1.2120,1.2150,1.2180. The last 2 digits 00-20-50-80. These areas are where you will find the magical Fractal and Breakouts. Repainting Fractals have nothing to do with anything , concerning a potential trade!!! All is based on SR levels and volume and where the price is headed.

Unless you understand what a Fractal represents and why they are on your chart, you are just lost.

I might add that the 21 EMA level is an essential point of concern and a Line in the Sand. A lot of decision making goes on when the currency price is at that level. A trend is usually established at that point, although the prices don't normally wonder to far away from that line in the sand. These Breakout are usually good for 30-80 pips on a 1 hour chart and take 5-6 hours to climax. I'm the conservative type, and usually take profit in the 30-40 pip range(2-3 hrs), with only a 15-20 SL in place. It gives me a 1:1.5 ratio, although it probably works out to be more like a 3:1 .

I trade a live account, wouldn't do it if I couldn't make money. I have traded Demo account and researched endless hours for the magical Indicators or an EA that would make some money. It's not out there Folks. It has to be in your Brain. You have to know what these Rascals are up to at all times. The trading does come easy now. I just set a Take Profit and a Stop Loss using 2% of my money trading a .15 lot for now and bring in a couple of trades a day, with very few losing trades. My Nest Egg will grow, but I really don't thing I have the nerve to trade anything more than a .5 lot size, regardless of my Bank Account size.A hundred Dollar Bill on the Stop Loss would be just about all I would what to surrender on any given trade. Still, at $5 pips and 50-60 pips / day, that will render @200-$300/day x21 days,-apprx. 30% tax with holding.

Alligator help determine the trend, and avoid ranging market, and Bill Williams Method helps on preventing impulsive trading because his system mostly using Stop Order. --- 帖子 #1501 ---
Very good question; too bad you never got an answer. I think just start off with the BW basics and be patient can pay off big time. For example, Fractals -

Fractals

Fractals generate the following signals:

• If a buy fractal is above the Alligator's teeth (the red line) we would place a Buy Stop one tick above the high of the up fractal;

• If a sell fractal is below the Alligator's teeth (the red line) we would place a Sell Stop one tick below the low of the fractal sell signal.

• We would not take a buy if a fractal is formed below the Alligator's teeth.

• We would not take a sell if a fractal is formed above the Alligator's teeth.

Fractals are valid until they are either triggered or a new fractal in the same direction appears (in this case the previous signal has to be ignored and the pending order has to be deleted).

I purchased Profitunity's course in the mid 2000's and studied and followed the methods intensely; also had regular conversations with Justine, Bills daughter.

I will paste a quote from another trader who used Bills method and used to be regular on this site, he also did the private mentoring.  "Dr. Bill Williams made some changes a few years ago. He does not use the AC or the Zone add-ons any longer. He uses just the AO and now the RSI only, set at 80/20 with a period of 9.

He also added another simple moving average (the purple line) set at 6 with a displacement at 3. This is used to exit. If you have 2 bars that close below the purple line, the exit would be one tick below the lowest bar (if long) or one tick above the highest bar (if short). You can also use the green line if a bar closes below (long) it or above it (short). He uses the purple line close as he says it can keep him in the trend longer which it does."

Trades can take anywhere between 1hour and 24hours to close and I don't use stops.

Easy pips traders.

--- 帖子 #1523 ---
Thanks.

No stops, I know it is not to every traders cup of tea but I hate them, I can't stand them.

If you buy in bullish with bill Williams it requires trailing stop or ATR to which I would only use ATR and it will be set at 4 to be taken of the candle prior to the break which is extremely accurate.

But like so many trading posts I read on fx factory this question always appears, &quot; where do I get out&quot;?

So by selling in bullish you have Ema's as targets. And by buying in bearish again you have EMA targets.

The fractal needs to be a good distance away from EMA, to begin with, and once a trade is placed I grid orders above if selling and below if buying usually 20-30 pips apart and  close trades at EMA,s this way I get 10 or so opportunitys for easy trades a day over multiple pairs.

Just set alerts at the break, receive an sms , place trade and orders, go for a coffee

--- 帖子 #1528 ---
The alligator was Bill's way of trying to get people to understand impulse vs. reaction. Don't trade reactive waves. Trade only impulse waves. Fibonacci, pivots, Murrey/Gann lines do not have any meaning in and of themselves, so you do not need to "trust" them.  They are just consistent lines in the sand so a trader can make decisions to trade off of. Any system of these kinds of indicators depends upon price action at it's core.

The AO is a 5/34 MACD and the AC is a 5 period moving average of the that MACD.

The zones concept is useful for money management techniques.

--- 帖子 #1532 ---
Context is by far the most difficult thing to teach with a trading method. If you are going use bill's methods, context is important.

Watch for trading opportunities when you are in a grey zone, start to see BDB bars, and a collapsing alligator. If you see a TF with an open alligator you are late. Wait until the alligator goes back to sleep.

Nothing in a chart is useless. Every bar gives information. What Bill did was to package well known market concepts into a course that newbies can take and understand.

I cannot say much about pyramiding. He has changed this a few time. I would just add a trading unit each time I get a signal.

In his first book he discussed air bag stops, not trades. Thumb trades were his early version of fractal trades.

--- 帖子 #1562 ---
The big misconception is that what makes the system successful are the indicators.  That is false.  The system is about adding on aggressively when a market breaks out and then trends.  So to do it properly, you need a sufficient account size to add-on and still not risk too much of the account.  So if you adhere to the rules 100%, you're adding on when each indicator gives a signal.  And each of the indicators have multiple setups for signals.

Having said that, the system was designed for daily charts during a period when markets only trended 15-20% of the time and the rest of the time were relatively flat.  Forex, obviously isn't like that.  So you'll need to find an instrument and timeframe where the indicators and setups make sense.  I found 15 min. charts and trading the London open to be the best.

--- 帖子 #1611 ---
Finally found a way to make "chaos money".

You need Dynamic trader software though!!

Here´s a weekly chart, AUDUSD.

DT has a swing file function, where you can create and manipulate swings. So first I create a swing file, using the oscillator as a guide.

Then I mark the last swing and using 2 statistical routines from the software, I let it plot time areas, where statistically 80% of the last say 10 swings, the trend changed (as well as the oscillator).

The routines are called Tyme Rythm Zones, and Time Bands. Those are the colored segments in the oscillator window below.

Then I draw a "time square", where both routines overlap in the future.

As you can see from the squares, drawn from the previous little colored arrows, and previous swings, those squares are quite accurate.I could show you dozens of similar hits.

Once the time is reached, I go to the daily chart, wait for a DIVERGENCE in the oscillator, and take the first divergence signal.

THEN, I add aggressively using the First Chaos edition Book techniques, (Zones/AO, AC, Balance Line, and fractals.)

And ride the wave till the next weekly square. I also use a lot of EW and Fibos in time and price. It just works.

Adding aggresively using chaos makes my winners bigger, and my losers (fewer lots entered), smaller.

--- 帖子 #1612 ---
Check this trade: AUDNZD, on a 12 Hour Bar (2 bars per day)

-Weekly OSC was OB

-Weekly Time Box was on (meaning statistical week swing high, time, was reached).

- WM1 Bar was DIVERGENT (very important filter, no divergence, no Wise Man in my book).

-After the first entry, I use BOTH BOOKS entries, all lots same size, same risk in $ to stop.

-WM1, WM2; WM3 from the second edition, AND all the other ones from the first edition.

-This campaign was 10 short entries, from the WM 1 till the place in the chart where I wrote "STOP adding."

-Once the daily Oscillator is OS (shown by the green bar below the DTF 8 oscillator, I stop adding positions.

-This trade was 10 entries altogether.

-Once the weekly Oscillator was OS, and I get a 12 H bullish oscillator reversal, I move my stop/TP to the top of that bar.

This move was approx. 8 times the pip profit than the whole move, would I have taken only one entry.

-My way of kkeping loosers small, winners big (the law number one in trading).

I trade 18 charts, mostly Forex, some commodities. Forex on 12 Hour charts, the others on Day charts.

Any time frame below is just too much stop running. Stop running happens even in the 12 hour. (nasty Big Boys ).

Just my 2 cents.

All the best.

Unless this is an advantage in the way that when you think you are reaching a high or low on your daily time frame then switch to a lower TF say 4 hours and wait for the cross of zero line signalling the beginning of a new wave or crossing its own SMA(5) signal line to exit from your trade or likewise prepare for the new one.

Furthermore I cannot still understand why the midpoint is used? Since the vast majority of the trading community is using the close of the session or time period also there are researches stressing on the importance of the closing price. Most of modern indicators, use EMAs on closing basis for smoothing why this one is using the SMA on midpoint, in his books he mentioned to have checked and tested the AO on mainframe computers he could do the same by checking the 5-34-5 EMA on closing basis which is same as 6-19-6 EMA on close devised by Gerald Appel for his buying signals! Since all these are more timely and give same indication for the wave 4 when it has to dive below or past above the zero line in order to be considered a valid 4th wave, or to see the divergent peak from wave 3 and 5!

I would not say that the Chaos 1st edition is strictly designed for daily TF though! The chaos 1st edition course is on YouTube please watch it is not offered anymore at profitunity.com ,  it is always combined with Elliott waves implying that you switch time frames so the wave you are looking at on your current time frame should have at least 90-120 candlesticks!

--- 帖子 #1631 ---
__________________________________________

EN:

Hello, I too am currently mastering Trade Chaos at the moment

What exactly do you not understand about MACD)?

If not to complicate and do unnecessary digging... in a nutshell, what I have heard and learned: Williams just took a simple math from the creator of MACD and applied it to his AO indicator, because it maximally coincided with his research and calculations.

He originally calculated all the readings for waves as in MFI, but it was very labor-intensive for computers of that time, so he took a simpler model for calculations, because it coincided with the original calculations.

As far as I've heard, the method moved towards simplification.

Eventually the three wise men came into being.

(although as they say, everything that was in the books - continues to work)

Angulation / 1st sage is really the most subjective element of all.

As Williams said, this is the moment when you have to break the rules (because it is an entry against the trend), but you have to know how to do it, because before you break the rules, you must first learn to follow the rules)))).

If I'm wrong about something, my elder brothers can correct me =)

__________________________________________

RU:

Здравствуйте, я тоже в данный момент осваиваю Торговый Хаос

Что именно вам непонятно с MACD?)

Если не усложнять и заниматься ненужными копаниями... в двух словах, что я слышал и узнал: Вильямс просто взял простую математическую систему от создателя MACD и применил ее для своего индикатора AO, т.к. она максимально совпадала с его исследованиями, расчётами.

Это же изначально все обстоятельства для волнового вычисления, как и в MFI, но это было очень трудозатратно для компьютеров того времени, поэтому он взял модель для расчётов проще, ведь она совпадала с внешними расчётами.

Сколько слышал, что метод двигался в сторону упрощения.

В конечном итоге появилось 3 мудреца.

(хотя как говорят, всё, что было в книгах - продолжает работать)

Ангуляция / 1й мудрец действительно, самый субъективный элемент из всех.

Как Вильямс, это тот момент когда надо нарушать правила(ведь это вход против тренда), однако это нужно уметь делать, ведь прежде чем нарушать, надо сначала выучить свои правила))))

Если вдруг в чём-то не прав, братья старшие могут поправить =)
